      <section class="module latest-news-module number-of-items-0">
       <h2 class="module-title">
        The Latest from
        <em>
         Science News
        </em>
       </h2>

        THE SOCIETY AND EDUCATION: GO DEEPER
       </p>
       <h2 class="module-title">
        Creating Access and Opportunities for Students and Teachers
       </h2>
       <div class="cards">
        <div class="picture-card">
         <a href="/outreach-and-equity/advocate-program/">
          <div class="image">
           <img alt="" class="orientation--lanscape" height="525" loading="lazy" sizes="(max-width: 960px) 100vw, 960px" src="https://www.societyforscience.org/wp-content/uploads/2019/08/advocate-_956.jpg" srcset="https://www.societyforscience.org/wp-content/uploads/2019/08/advocate-_956.jpg 965w, https://www.societyforscience.org/wp-content/uploads/2019/08/advocate-_956-300x164.jpg 300w, https://www.societyforscience.org/wp-content/uploads/2019/08/advocate-_956-768x420.jpg 768w" width="960"/>
          </div>
          <div class="card-body">
           <h3 class="card-title">
            Advocate Program
           </h3>
           <div class="card-description wysiwyg">
            <p>
             Discover how we build STEM access by helping mentors of underrepresented and low-income students entering research projects in scientific or engineering competitions.
            </p>
           </div>
          </div>
         </a>
        </div>
        <div class="picture-card">
         <div class="image">
          <img alt="" class="orientation--lanscape" height="500" loading="lazy" sizes="(max-width: 900px) 100vw, 900px" src="https://www.societyforscience.org/wp-content/uploads/2019/09/cover.jpg" srcset="https://www.societyforscience.org/wp-content/uploads/2019/09/cover.jpg 900w, https://www.societyforscience.org/wp-content/uploads/2019/09/cover-300x167.jpg 300w, https://www.societyforscience.org/wp-content/uploads/2019/09/cover-768x427.jpg 768w, https://www.societyforscience.org/wp-content/uploads/2019/09/cover-740x411.jpg 740w" width="900"/>
         </div>
         <div class="card-body">
          <h3 class="card-title">
           Research Teachers Conferences
          </h3>
          <div class="card-description wysiwyg">
           <p>
            Learn how the
            <a href="https://www.societyforscience.org/outreach-and-equity/high-school-research-teachers-conference/">
             High School Research Teachers Conference
            </a>
            and our new
            <a href="https://www.societyforscience.org/outreach-and-equity/middle-school-research-teachers-conference/">
             Middle School Research Teachers Conference
            </a>
            bring educators together for what one participant called “the best professional development experience of my career.”
           </p>
          </div>
         </div>
        </div>
        <div class="picture-card">
         <a href="/outreach-and-equity/science-news-in-high-schools/">

          </div>
          <div class="card-body">
           <h3 class="card-title">
            <i>
             Science News
            </i>
            in High Schools
           </h3>
